<h2>All Reviews</h2>

<ol>
    <li> Cheers to Braun&#x27;s innovation in addressing the age-old problem of electric shavers with its cutting element generating heat whilst shaving. The \\&quot;Active Cooling\\&quot; feature instantly activates the cool strip in between the two (2) cutting elements, which actually provides a soothing, cool feeling on your skin during the shave. My older Braun 1775 shaver is still working after 9 years but decided to upgrade and try the new Braun CoolTec CT5cc model. Although it&#x27;s a bit chunkier, I like the fact that the two (2) independent cutting elements improves coverage and precision, cutting more hair in less time, giving me a closer shave. To top it all off, the base included in the kit doubles up as a charger and a built-in cleaning station which uses a bluish solution, similar to the ones used in salons to disinfect their cutting tools, and with one push of the button, it cleans and disinfects the razor head. That is definitely cool.</li>
    <li> Pound and wasn&#x27;t happy with the shave</li>
    <li> For the most part it gets a pretty close shave and the CoolTech system works great, but the actual shaver doesn&#x27;t seem to get every hair on your face. I had trouble with areas on my face and neck that the shaver would not shave off. I would go over the same spot multiple times in different directions and it still wold not get as close as the rest of my face or neck. I didn&#x27;t expect it to be perfect but I expected it to work a little better than it did.</li>
    <li> I tried this shaver for a week, and while the cooling part of the unit is a very interesting effect, the fact that the head does not pivot really limited my ability to get a close shave.  After a week, I was reaching for my old Braun instead of this.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Also note that because it comes with the cleaning solution, you apparently cannot return this to Amazon.  Still working through the details with them on how to resolve.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I have used several Braun models over the years, including the series 7, which in my opinion is their best model.  This one is definitely a step backwards from that.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Just a quick update - Amazon resolved the return process quickly and simply.</li>
    <li> I was very excited to try my new Braun CoolTec electric shaver and was not disappointed. I was blown away by how smooth the shave was and how cool my face stayed throughout the shave. I was not itchy or irritated during or after the shaving process (which is not always true with other razors). The razor is solid, but flexible at the same time to give a smooth shave that gets every aspect of the face.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The Clean&amp;Charge Station was really cool and something I have not seen before. I like knowing my shaver is clean before each use.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The electric shaver was provided via a program run by Braun.</li>
    <li> Coming from a guy with sensitive skin, I can&#x27;t say enough about this CoolTec system. The cooling bar is unbelievable. I wondered to myself before I tried it what benefit this would bring to the table. It really is an enjoyable feel to have a cool shave, when activated. I say when activated because this system allows you to turn the cool bar on and off. In addition, I always hated to clean my dry shave razor. With the CoolTec system, you can clean and charge this shaver with the push of a button by putting the razor in the cleaning station. The CoolTec system also comes with a travel case and travel lock feature to prevent it from turning on in your luggage-how cool is that!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I received this shaver through a program with Braun and I&#x27;m so happy I decided to try it!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I would recommend this shaver to any guy that&#x27;s looking for an easy to maintain razor that leaves you with a clean smooth shave every time!</li>
    <li> I received this Braun&#x27;s Â°CoolTec electric shaver as part of a program Braun was doing. When I first received it I was highly impressed.  The idea of it was pretty \\&quot;cool\\&quot;, however after using for a week or so I am less than impressed.  I know this is an electric razor but it didn&#x27;t get into the hard to reach contours in my face.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I also am not crazy about having to buy replacement cooling packs.  It says that they only last about 3-4 weeks on the packaging.  I don&#x27;t want to have to remember to buy \\&quot;extras\\&quot; for this so I don&#x27;t know if I would recommend just based on this.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Over all it was just an okay razor, but not the best out there.</li>
    <li> I was very excited to receive the Braun CoolTec Shaver after  hearing that it reduces shaving irritation.  While I was in the Navy, I had to shave twice a day, if I had duty.  Having to shave every day, irritates my face to no end.  I was hoping that this would be the razor that fixed this problem.  I loved the razor itself and how easy it was to handle.  I became disappointed after I started shaving.  i had to go over my chin and neck several times, which irritated my skin.  I was hoping to shave once, get all the hair and no irritation.  No luck.  Braun&#x27;s sent the Braun CootTec Shaver to get my opinion of the shaver and I hate to say that for the money it would cost to buy, I think you could purchase a better razor for less money.  The other issue was the price of the replacement blade.  It was a little more costly than others.  I did find that the battery charge held.  I truly wanted to like this razor, but I don&#x27;t think it&#x27;s worth the cost.</li>
    <li> I got the shaver for free from Braun for a program it is running. I have to say I&#x27;m impressed with it.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I can feel that it is cool to the touch. I have always used a Gillette Mach 3 standard razor and this is way better. I get pretty bad razor burn on my neck from a conventional razor and after using the Braun on two consecutive days I havent had a problem. I even did my head (disclaimer...there wasn&#x27;t much hair left) and it worked great.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;It is super convenient to simply throw it on the charger after using it and just by pressing a button it cleans it out.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I did have an issue with a spot just above my ear. It would touch the spot because of the contour of my head and the extending trimmer didn&#x27;t really work well either.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;***Update***&lt;br /&gt;Ive had a chance to use the system for a while and I was less impressed over time.  Im not sure if it is all electric razors but the shave never got close to the skin and missed a lot on my face.  I felt like I had to go over the area multiple times in order for it to get razor close.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I have been using my normal multiple blade razor the beginning of my work week and hitting the electric razor half way through.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;It is still good at not irritating my skin and have even used it on my head a few times.  It actually seemed to work better on my head than it did on my face.</li>
    <li> I received my Braun CoolTec electric razor on 11/12/13 which was provided via a program run by Braun.  I tried it out and I must say it is really a &amp;#34;cool&amp;#34; tech product. The metal bar in the middle of the blades is very cold and makes your skin feel cool and not so rough and worn out.  It has 3 options to be cleaned which are 1. Manually with the included brush. 2. Take blade off and rinse it under the water or 3. You can just put the electric razor inside the self cleaning device and will clean,sterilize and lubricate it for the next time of use.  Also final feature is how quick it charges from the time it is put on the charger and charges under an hour.  I highly recommend this product and I am very satisfied with it.  I will never go back to any kind of razor blades again.</li>
    <li> I tried the Braun CoolTec electric shaver through a program run by Braun and I was a little skeptical.  How much difference could a cold little bar make?  Well I was wrong.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I gave it a try and was pleasantly surprised by the performance of the razor.  The razor does a very nice job and the CoolTec cooling bar did a very nice job soothing my skin.  I did not have any red razor burns on my face which is common with all other electric razors I have tried.  Additionally, the cleaning station was a really cool added bonus.  With the touch of a button, the charging/cleaning station takes care of all the messy cleaning and it will be ready to use, clean and charged, the next day.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;As a small negative, the Braun CoolTec does not get as close of a shave as a traditional razor and shaving cream.  But I have not found a single electric razor that does.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Overall, I was really impressed with the Braun CoolTec electric razor.  Together with the charging/cleaning station and the soft case that will allow me to take this on the road with me, I think this is a great razor for a close shave without any skin irritation.</li>
    <li> Great shaver the cooling factor is something else it truly makes for a better shaving.  Braun offered this to me to try out and have to say it is the best electric shaver i have ever used.  Deffinatlly would recommend this to everyone its one nice shaver and works very very well</li>
    <li> I was able to try out the new Braun CoolTec Shaver through a program run by Braun.  I&#x27;ve used a lot of shaving brands and products in my adult life, and this might be one of my new favorites.  The product itself comes with the shaver, traveling case, power cord, and charging/cleaning station.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I used the shaver a couple of days ago and it did a great job.  I had a full beard, so I used the built-in trimmer to bring my beard down to stubble.  I then used the CoolTec Shaver to make my face silky smooth.  The CoolTec Technology exceeded my expectations.  I didn&#x27;t have that awful burning feeling I get when I&#x27;ve used other shavers.  Once I was done I put it on the cleaning base to have it cleaned for the next shave, and it charges at the same time.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I highly recommend the Braun CoolTec Shaver.  My only negative is that, like with many other shavers, it was very tricky getting some of those pesky hairs that refused to be trimmed.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This is a great product, and for any guy looking for a new shaver, this is the one.</li>
    <li> I received my Braun Cooltec in the mail a few days ago. When i found out that Braun would be sending me one to try out i was super stoked. Right out of the package you can tell that this is not your typical electric razor. It comes with a a clean and charge station that not only recharges the razor in between uses but also cleans the blades and lubricates them to keep them in tip top shape. After a quick charge I had to give this razor a try. The first thing I noticed was the cooling feature, where an aluminum cooling bar is chilled to reduce irritation. I was a little skeptical at first but was pleasantly surprised as to how well it cools. I have to say that it gave me one of the best shaves i have ever had using an electric razor. Absolutely no irritation and a very close shave. I actually had my wife feel the side of my face after shaving, suffice it say she approves. I would definitely recommend this razor to people that are looking for a great electric razor that gives a very close shave without the irritation.</li>
    <li> I&#x27;m newer to electronic shavers as I usually use clippers to maintain my facial hair. However, I was surprised by the performance of this product. I enjoyed the cooling function, that was pretty awesome. I also managed to get a pretty close shave as well. While I won&#x27;t be switching over completely to electric shavers due to the length I tend to keep my facial hair, I will definitely break this out when I need to get close.</li>
    <li> My husband loves it. Clearer is hard to find though and expensive</li>
    <li> First, I&#x27;d like to start off by saying that I don&#x27;t have a thick beard, so I can&#x27;t say that I did a good job of stress testing the razor.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Next, I&#x27;d like to say that the razor does work well.  It&#x27;s a very comfortable shave and the cooling mechanism works noticeably well.  Granted, I can shave without it and experience no irritation, but it does feel better to have it on.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Unfortunately, I wasn&#x27;t impressed with the performance.  For my first shave, I let my beard grow as long as I normally do for about a week.  It doesn&#x27;t grow very fast.  While it did cut most of the hairs, it did leave a few stubborn hairs that were laying down. Before you use it, you have to open a cartridge that contains or what seems to smell like rubbing alcohol and insert it in.  Really easy.  The cartridge does need to be replaced and there is an indicating light that tells you when it does. What this allows you to do is after each shave, you can place the razor in an accompanying base which will automatically clean and charge the razor. This removes an maintenance you may need to do (other than the 18 month blade change) because the shaver is cleaned and lubricated after each shave. It should be noted that these cleaning cartridges do run about $1 USD each week, so it is an investment. In lieu of this, you can clean the shave under running water and invest in a bottle of Shaver Saver to get the same results but with more manual intervention. Overall the shave base is nice in that my sink real estate is saved a bit by sprawling cords and shaver parts drying all over the place, and I feel the investment is worth it.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Price&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The price component is a big differentiator for many, with nearly a $100 USD difference between the two razors.&lt;br /&gt;What you will find is that the Series 7 is the Lexus of the group, with very fast performance, extra bells and whistles (three modes of shaving), and nicer aesthetics. This razor is excellent and honestly you can&#x27;t go wrong selecting this on a deal.&lt;br /&gt;The CoolTec shaver is very much a specialty razor. Essentially you will get the same results as a Series 7 because the foil is very similar. The difference will be in shaving time because of the slower motor on the CoolTec. What you gain is the ability to cool your face downand greatly increase comfort during the shaving process. This makes for one of the only electric shavers today tailor made for those with sensitive skin.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Summary&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;To summarize, Braun has a real winner here and a very big product differentiator from competitors. Being that the CoolTec is essentially a Series 3 with a cooling module, I can see them putting this feature on all Series models in future iterations because it works so well. Braun packages this German-made shaver very well and includes Carrying Case, Cleaning Base, Fluid, and Shaver. Of the 15+ shavers I have used in my lifetime (and some manual shaving too), this razor is by far the best because instead of making the motors bigger and faster, Braun decided to focus on comfort as well. Not having to spend countless dollars on aftershave/lotion alone makes this razor a great return on investment. Should you not like the razor, Braun does offer a 60-day return period, but I doubt you will need it!</li>

    <li> I received the Braun CoolTec shaver via a program run by Braun.  It came at the perfect time, as I was about ready to replace my more than 10 year old Braun Synchro 7505.  My experience with the Braun CoolTec shaver was both positive and negative.  Let me break it down for you.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;WHAT&#x27;S GOOD?&lt;br /&gt;The main selling point of the CoolTech is that it&#x27;s the \\&quot;World&#x27;s 1st shaver with active cooling technology\\&quot;.  This feature is designed to cool your skin and reduce irritation.  I found that this feature worked great.  When you turn on the cooling feature, an electro-ceramic cooling element cools the skin as you shave.  It cools quickly, works remarkably well and delivers the benefit it advertises.  Every time I used the shaver my skin was left irritation free and it gave me a more comfortable shave than other shavers I have tried.  This cooling feature does come with a tradeoff, which I&#x27;ll get to later on.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Braun claims that the adaptable 3-stage cutting system provides a closer shave.  They&#x27;re spot on.  When comparing the shave I got from the CoolTech to the shave I have been getting from my Synchro - there&#x27;s no contest.  The CoolTech shaves closer and smoother.  Certainly that&#x27;s a feature that you&#x27;re looking for in an electric shaver and this shaver has it.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;And here&#x27;s another positive: all the hair stays inside the head of the shaver!  I mention this because so many electric shavers \\&quot;leak\\&quot; shavings all over your sink and counter (my Synchro does).  The Braun CoolTech traps all shavings in the head until you&#x27;re ready to dump them.  Nice!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;WHAT&#x27;S NOT SO GOOD?&lt;br /&gt;While the active cooling technology is great and it does its job well, it comes at a cost.  The cooling element is (as you might expect) sandwiched directly in between the main cutting elements.  This \\&quot;gap\\&quot; between the blades makes for wider shaver head and an odd sensation especially when shaving up near the ears or below the nose.  It feels that the shave would be more efficient if the two blades were together.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I was never quite sure how to hold the shaver.  I must have rotated it twenty times while shaving just to see 1) the most comfortable way to hold it and 2) the way to hold it that gets me the best shave.  I have still not yet determined the answer to this conundrum but I will say this:  It&#x27;s not the most comfortable shaver to use.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The long-hair trimmer may well be the worst aspect of the shaver.  It&#x27;s pretty much useless.  The lack of power to the trimmer made it impossible to trim my sideburn (not thick at all).  To test the trimmer (and to make sure it was actually getting power), I touched it to a piece of cardboard.  It made almost no mark.  You simply cannot use this trimmer at all.  That means you&#x27;ll need a second sculpting razor handy.  That&#x27;s a big negative.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The Braun CoolTech package comes with a cleaning station similar to those that Braun has been using for several years.  This was my first experience with the cleaning station and I found it to be very good.  It cleaned the razor in about 3 minutes and allowed for a great place to charge the unit as well.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;SUMMARY&lt;br /&gt;Having used the Synchro for over 10 years, it will take some getting used to using the CoolTech, but I&#x27;m planning on making that happen.  I have had excellent results with Braun products and I have no reason to believe that, if properly taken care of, this CoolTech shaver will last me many years.  It&#x27;s hard for me to say that this is an excellent product due to the drawbacks I&#x27;ve mentioned above but the unique cooling technology is a great feature.  If Braun were to change just a couple other things about this shaver, it would have a superior product on its hands.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;UPDATE: 12/17/13&lt;br /&gt;Having used this shaver for several weeks now, I have upped my rating to 4/5 stars.  The shaver really does deliver all it says it will.  It keeps the skin cool and provided a close, smooth shave.  I have gotten used to the weight of the shaver (heavier than many) and the split shaving head (split by the cooling ceramic).  The cleaning system works perfectly - cleaning the shaver back to out-of-the-box condition.  The long-hair trimmer is still the weakest part of this shaver.  It&#x27;s pretty powerless.  The CoolTech is nice, quality shaving system and is definitely worth a look should you be on the market for a new shaver.d to the weight of the shaver (heavier than many) and the split shaving head (split by the cooling ceramic). The flip side of this is even with the hair a little longer, there is less pulling on the hair as it shaves than there was with the Norelco.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;In conclusion, yes, I like this razor, and I would recommend it and have recommended it to friends. I still think it beats the pants off of of my Norelco (though to be fair, it&#x27;s a little older model.) I don&#x27;t know if it&#x27;s the circular vs. strait blades, the CoolTec or a newer model, but what I do know is I have MUCH less skin irritation, especially on my neck and for me that is a VERY big deal. It is very weak, and doesn&#x27;t do a good job for precision cutting.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;If I go a few days between shaves, this thing is pretty much useless.     <li> So, I&#x27;ve been a loyal Braun customer for many, many years. My current Braun doesn&#x27;t have a fancy cooling bar, but it does a great job with my morning shave, so I was interested to see how well the new Braun CoolTec system worked in comparison.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;My Braun CoolTec system was provided to me via a program run by Braun, so my financial investment wasn&#x27;t a consideration, as it would be for others.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;On the whole, I would recommend the Braun CoolTec to a family member or friend if they have a little more to invest in their shaver system - short term and long-term.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Short-term, the CoolTec doesn&#x27;t necessarily warrant an upgrade if you already had a great Braun shaver.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Long-term, the Clean&amp;Charge station, while providing some healthy conditioning of the shaver, is a long-term expense, too. I used to have a Remington shaver, and cleaning was more tedious due to the way the motor assembly attached to the shaver head, and it really tore up my pores.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;As I&#x27;ve never experienced redness or irritation with my previous Braun, I wouldn&#x27;t be inclined to recommend the Braun CoolTec system if it doesn&#x27;t solve an existing problem. If I did experience redness or irritation, I can see how the really &amp;#34;cool&amp;#34; cooling bar might help, and the 3-stage cutting system might be a more comfortable shave. However, the end result - a smooth, clean shave - is achievable with most Braun shavers.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;So, before buying a Braun CoolTec system, consider whether the great new cooling bar technology will solve an issue you might have with redness and irritation. Also, consider your budget and the great many other Braun models available at a lower cost.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I&#x27;m giving the Braun CoolTec shaver a 4-star rating because it&#x27;s yet another Braun shaver system to consider favorably against other options.</li>

    <li> It&#x27;s not what I was expecting but it&#x27;s ok!</li>
    <li> In my 25 years of shaving, I&#x27;ve seen a lot of gimmicks come and go and most of them really didn&#x27;t add anything to the shave. Braun&#x27;s CoolTec is different.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;For the past year I have been dry shaving with the highly rated top-of-the line Norelco Sensotouch 3D 1080x and I have never really been satisfied with it, especially for the price. The shave has never been very close, and I found the rotary heads somewhat irritating. By chance one day I came across the Braun CoolTec shaver in a local big-box store and was instantly intrigued by the active cooling technology. I really didn&#x27;t want to drop the cash on another high-end shaver after investing in the Norelco but the CoolTec was just calling to me. A few days later I found it on sale at a good price and bought it on impulse, fully expecting another gimmicky razor with a mediocre shave that would be returned shortly thereafter. Boy, was I wrong. From the first shave I found it faster, closer and definitely more comfortable than the Norelco.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;In the box you&#x27;ll find the razor, cleaning station, power cord, zippered travel case, charging cradle, one Clean and Renew cartridge, cleaning brush and manual.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The cooling bar really does cut down on irritation and just plain feels good on the skin. It&#x27;s hard to describe the sensation...it&#x27;s not ice-cold, but it&#x27;s like rubbing a cold spoon on your face. It does take a few seconds for it to reach maximum coldness so I start with my cheeks before moving to the more sensitive areas on the neck. It should be noted that using the CoolTec feature does cut down on battery life, but if you recharge after frequently it&#x27;s really not an issue. Pushing the \\&quot;snowflake\\&quot; button toggles it on and off, and I like that the razor remembers this setting when you turn it off. After shaving with the CoolTec feature, I honestly feel like I don&#x27;t even need aftershave balm.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The only other button is the power button, which also glows to indicate the battery level. Green when it&#x27;s full, red when it&#x27;s getting low. There is also an LED indicator that lights when the razor needs cleaning, and another that tells you when it&#x27;s travel locked. Fit and finish are excellent, and the lacquer finish is very nice (I got the blue version). The razor is a bit on the large size, but feels very good in the hand. Unlike other reviewers, I don&#x27;t find that I need too many passes for a good shave, a lot fewer than the Norelco in fact. I also owned a Panasonic Arc 4 before the Norelco, and I would say the Braun CoolTec shaves nearly on par with the Panasonic and much closer than the Norelco. Having said that, keep in mind that every guy&#x27;s beard is different and your mileage may vary.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I haven&#x27;t used the pop-up trimmer very much yet, but it gets the job done. Again, much better than the tiny slide-out trimmer on the Norelco. This shaver is also waterproof, so you can use it in the shower if you like. I prefer to shave dry before showering.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The cleaning station works well and leaves the razor with a fresh, clean scent. I really like that there is a soft \\&quot;beep\\&quot; sound that lets you know the razor is properly seated in the base. I have heard others complain about the cost of refills, but each refill is only about $5-$6 and lasts a month or more. For me, around a buck a week is a small price to pay for a clean, sanitized razor every day. Not to mention it also lubricates the blades which makes them last longer. Speaking of blades, the replacement cartridge for the razor is quite a bit cheaper than the Sensotouch 3D replacement and is rated to last 18 months rather than 12.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;This razor may not have all the bells and whistles of the 790cc or Sensotouch 3D 1080x models, but I have finally come to the realization that I don&#x27;t need those...all I really need is a great shave and the CoolTec delivers.reen when it&#x27;s full, red when it&#x27;s getting low. There is also an LED indicator that lights when the razor needs cleaning, and another that tells you when it&#x27;s travel locked. Fit and finish are excellent, and the lacquer finish is very nice (I got the blue version). The razor is a bit on the large size, but feels very good in the hand. Unlike other reviewers, I don&#x27;t find that I need too many passes for a good shave, a lot fewer than the Norelco in fact. I also owned a Panasonic Arc 4 before the Norelco, and I would say the Braun CoolTec shaves nearly on par with the Panasonic and much closer than the Norelco. Having said that, keep in mind that every guy&#x27;s beard is different and your mileage may vary.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I haven&#x27;t used the pop-up trimmer very much yet, but it gets the job done.     <li> I&#x27;ll preface by saying that I had virtually no experience with electric razors prior to this product. I owned a three-head Norelco from over 10 years ago that was horrible...I had been using blades until I received this as a gift a year ago.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;First, I&#x27;ll preface by saying if you want any type of facial hair (beard/stubble, chin strap, goatee, etc.) this product will be useless for you. The pop-up trimmer is only appropriate for evening out sideburns; precision facial hair detailing simply cannot be accomplished with this razor.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Aesthetically, the razor looks great. It feels solid and sturdy, and is comfortable to hold. It looks really cool in its cleaning base, as well, sitting there looking like the sword in the stone when you&#x27;re not using it. That cleaning solution does its job really well too; the foil feels great after being cleaned, and on top of that it comes out smelling like lemons, which is awesome. Battery life is a non-issue; you&#x27;ll have more than enough juice to get you through even a lengthy shave (which is one of this razor&#x27;s main downsides...more on that later).&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The main selling point of this Braun is the CoolTec system. Basically, an aluminum element situated between the cutting foils gradually becomes cooler as you shave. It actually works great. The cooling sensation feels pleasant on the skin, and there&#x27;s definitely less irritation than the old Norelco that I previously used. Since its an electric, you won&#x27;t be nicking or cutting your skin as you shave, either. After about 15-20 minutes, however, the cooling element will cease functioning and need to be...erm...cooled down before being used again. That&#x27;s not a deal-breaker, though, and overall, this product provides the most comfortable shave I&#x27;ve ever had, and for that it deserves praise.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;What is a deal breaker is the quality of the shave you get from this product. This is going to be subjective, since everyone&#x27;s facial hair grows differently (directionof hair growth, rate of hair growth, thickness/coarseness, etc). My facial hair grows in pretty quickly and relatively coarse.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Firstly, if you have anything more than a two-day old beard, this thing in general is going to be miserable unless you trim down your stubble first. The quality of the shave is quite uneven and immensely disappointing. The shaver does well on the cheeks/jaw and chin, and does an okay job on the upper lip area (provided you use a blade to get the hairs just under your nose). However, it fails miserable in the area underneath the chin, and on the neck. There are always a handful of hairs and/or clusters of stubble that seem to be outside of the shaver&#x27;s ability, even after multiple passes. I&#x27;ve tried shaving dry and using Lectric Shave, and I still have the same problem. You may need to follow up with a pass of a traditional blade to ensure closeness, which kind of defeats the purpose. This increases your shaving time to inconvenient lengths.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I&#x27;m not going to say this is a bad product. The cleaning base and CoolTec functionality are wonderful features to have in an electric shaver, and they really do work as advertised. The shave is serviceable (if uneven), which isn&#x27;t bad, but you&#x27;d expect more from this relatively expensive electric shaver.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;If you want a clean-shaven look, and as long as you shave every day (every other day at the most), you&#x27;ll be okay with this razor and may even love it. Everyone else should approach this product with caution. One year later, I still use mine sporadically when I want the aforementioned clean-shaven look and don&#x27;t want to nick up my face. At all other times, I&#x27;ll be using a blade.</li>

Upon inspection of the cutting head, it is as clean as before i used it.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Final thoughts:&lt;br /&gt;I am going to use the crap out of this during summer (too bad its November now). It also comes with a self cleaning unit that does the trick and keeps it sparkling and sanitary. The Braun CoolTec system is incredibly simple and easy to use.  For the most part, it just involves pressing a few buttons!     <li> I&#x27;ve gone through multiple electric shavers since my first shaver was handed down to me from my dad when my beard just started coming in at the ripe old age of 8...ok maybe 15.  That first shaver was awesome, it signified my transition to manhood, but it was ultimately a heaping pile of junk and soon replaced with a regular razor as it just did not give as close or as quick a shave.  Since then every shaver I&#x27;ve had was not able to compete with a razor on quickness or smoothness of shave so I was skeptical when Braun offered me the chance to review the CoolTec Men&#x27;s shaver for free, but hey it&#x27;s free right, so why not give it a chance.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;The first thing I noticed about the shaver was the price, almost $200 retail?!  It better be good for that price!  The next thing I noticed when I received my package was the bulkiness of the cleaning station (my bathroom is currently very small and I share it with my wife, enough said).  Well I set it up and let it clean the razor, it was a bit loud but pretty quick.  I then sadly used the trimmer on my epic beard I had grown over Movember, which was oddly satisfying for my wife, and was pleased with the smoothness and effectiveness of the trimmer.  I was also impressed with the weight and feel of the shaver in my hand, it felt very comfortable and solid, like if I dropped it on the tile it would be fine, not the cheap light plastic feel I was expecting.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Ok the trimmer works great, that&#x27;s nice but not terribly surprising.  I flipped on the cooling feature of the razor since it is the cornerstone of the product and began my shave.  The cooling kicked in almost immediately and provided a marked difference to the feel of the shaver against my skin.  It was refreshing and kept my skin from sticking to the shaver and my hair from getting pulled.  The fact that the shaver was also freshly cleaned was noticeable as well, it kept the blades very smooth and lubricated, unlike any electric shaver I had experienced previously, even when freshly cleaned with a third party lubricating agent.  The shave went relatively fast and I did not find myself needing to go over many areas repeatedly, except for a few small trouble areas.  Once the shave was complete I was honestly amazed with how close and smooth of a shave I had received from an electric shaver.  I would say it was about 95% as good as the best manual razor I&#x27;ve used, which was miles ahead of any other shaver I have experienced previously, and there was almost no irritation, which again, was unexpected and impressive.  Next came cleanup.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Cleaning the shaver was a cinch.  The head pops right off and is easily rinsed, as is the shaver itself.  Putting the head back on was just as easy and popping it on the cleaning station for a fresh, complete clean was a snap, much easier than other razors that you need to disassemble piece by piece, then lubricate with a spray or other third party agent, then most likely next time you use will need to apply a pre-electric shave gel or other prepping agent.  Not that you couldn&#x27;t do that with the CoolTec shaver but I really don&#x27;t see a need to.  Storing the razor safely is easy with the travel case and docking station provided.  Storing the cleaning station is a bit more of a challenge as the cleaning agent in the system can spill if it is tilted too much, but the plug and cord detach which is good for storage and I found a nice spot under my sink to set the system until next time.  I would definitely recommend using the cleaning station after every use to get the closest, smoothest shave out of your Braun CoolTec shaver.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Overall I was completely amazed with the quality of shave and ease of use of the Braun CoolTec shaver and my expectations, low as they were, were far exceeded.  I would say this shaver gave the best electric shave I have ever experienced.  That being said I still think using a quality manual razor is faster and gives a slightly cleaner shave, although thecost of replacements can be steep and will eventually exceed the cost of this system if you require frequent shaving for your job or other reason.  I won&#x27;t be putting away my razors just yet but for travelling and for a quick touch up the Braun CoolTec Shaver is miles ahead of other shavers if you can get over the price and have a little bit of storage under your sink!  It&#x27;s definitely worth the price.</li>
